m.deaths : (ageTabV == 2) ? m.tested : m.count}),\n            text: selectedRows.map(function (m) { return m[(ageTabV == 1) ? \'deaths\' : (ageTabV == 2) ? \'tested\' : \'count\'] }),\n            hovertemplate: \'%{y:,d}\',\n            mode: \'none\',\n            name: \'Total\'\n        };\n        dataGrp.push(dataTotals);\n        var dataAgeburst = dataGrp;\n        Plotly.react(\'pieAge\', dataAgeburst, unpack(selectedRows, (ageTabV == 2) ? \'tested\' : \'count\').reduce(function (a, b) { return a + b }) > 0 ? layoutagepie : layoutNoData, { responsive: true });\n    }\n    function populateRaceChartValues(selectedRows) {\n        var dataRace = [{\n            type: \'pie\',\n            labels: unpack(selectedRows, \'description\'),\n            values: unpack(selectedRows, (raceTabV == 1) ? \'deaths\' : (raceTabV == 2) ? \'tested\' : \'count\'),\n            marker: { colors: unpack(selectedRows, \'color\') },\n            textposition: \'outside\',\n            automargin: true,\n            textinfo: \'label+value\',\n        }];\n        Plotly.react(\'pieRace\', dataRace, unpack(selectedRows, (raceTabV == 2) ? \'tested\' : \'count\').reduce(function (a, b) { return a + b }) > 0 ? layoutrace : layoutNoData, { responsive: true });\n    }\n    function populateGenderChartValues(selectedRows) {\n        var dataGender = [{\n            type: \'pie\',\n            labels: unpack(selectedRows, \'description\'),\n            values: unpack(selectedRows, (genderTabV == 1) ? \'deaths\' : (genderTabV == 2) ? \'tested\' : \'count\'),\n            marker: { colors: unpack(selectedRows, \'color\') },\n            automargin: true,\n            textinfo: \'label+value\',\n        }];\n\n        Plotly.react(\'pieGender\', dataGender, unpack(selectedRows, (genderTabV == 2) ? \'tested\' : \'count\').reduce(function (a, b) { return a + b }) > 0 ? layoutpie : layoutNoData, { responsive: true });\n    }\n    function updateCounty() {\n        setCountySelection(selectCounty.value);\n    }\n    selectCounty.addEventListener(\'change\', updateCounty, false);\n        function linkCounty(selectedCounty) {\n        selectCounty.value = selectedCounty;\n        setCountySelection(selectedCounty);\n    }\n    function setCountySelection(selectedCounty) {\n        selectedC = selectedCounty;\n        populateAgeChart(0);\n        populateRaceChart(0);\n        populateGenderChart(0);\n    }\n\n//--><!]]>\n</script></div></div></div>\n</article>\n</div>\n<aside class="sidebars">\n<section
